THE   CUSTOMS  ORDINANCE
Order under Section 19A
BY virtue of the power vested in me under Section 19(A) of the Customs Ordinance (Chapter 235) as amended by
Customs (Amendment) Law No. 35 of 1974 and Customs (Amendment) Act, No. 83 of 1988, I, Mangala Samaraweera,
Minister of Finance do by this Order exempt the goods specified in Column V of the Schedule hereto, imported by or
consigned to the persons or institutions specified in the corresponding entry in Column II of that Schedule from such
amount of the duties of Customs leviable thereon as are specified in the corresponding entry in Column VIII of that
Schedule subject to the condition that the importer or person by whom or on whose behalf the goods are sold or disposed
of country to the condition of the Order shall prior to such sale or disposal obtain the permission of the Direcor General
of Customs and pay the duties payable on such goods at the time of such sale or disposal to the Director General of
Customs in terms of Section 19(A) Sub-section (3).
If any goods are sold or disposed of contrary to the condition of the Order without the prior permission of the
Director General of Customs, The importer or consignee shall be leviable to pay the full duties of Customs leviable
thereon at the time of importation. Such goods shall also be leviable to be forfeited under Section 19(A) Sub-section (3).
M
ANGALA  S AMARAWEERA ,
Minister of Finance.
Ministry of Finance,
Colombo 01,
30th September, 2019.
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A -  PG   4664— 467  (10/2019)
